<script type="text/javascript">
  var headerEl = document.getElementsByClassName('header-r23');
  if (headerEl.length > 0) {
    headerEl = headerEl[0];

    // popolamento parametri header (modifier) - viene fatto via js in modo che non vada in cache

    var headerAlignCenter = false;    
    var headerInitialColor = 'black';
    var headerInitialBackground = 'white';

    if (typeof coremediaR23Settings !== 'undefined') {            
      if (typeof coremediaR23Settings.headerAlignCenter !== 'undefined') {
    	  headerAlignCenter = coremediaR23Settings.headerAlignCenter;
		  }
      
      if (typeof coremediaR23Settings.headerInitialColor !== 'undefined') {
        switch (coremediaR23Settings.headerInitialColor) {
          case 'white':
            headerInitialColor = 'white';
            break;
          case 'black':
          default:
            headerInitialColor = 'black';
            break;
        }    	  
		  }

      if (typeof coremediaR23Settings.headerInitialBackground !== 'undefined') {
        switch (coremediaR23Settings.headerInitialBackground) {
          case 'transparent':
          case 'dark-gradient':
          case 'light-gradient':
            headerInitialBackground = coremediaR23Settings.headerInitialBackground;
            break;
          case 'white':
          default:
            headerInitialBackground = 'white';
            break;
        }
		  }
    }    
        
    if (headerAlignCenter) {
      headerEl.classList.add('header-r23--vcenter', 'header-r23--scroll-down');
    }

    headerEl.setAttribute('data-initial-color', headerInitialColor);
    headerEl.setAttribute('data-initial-background', headerInitialBackground);
    
    var headerAlert = document.getElementsByClassName('header__alert--r23');
    if (headerAlert.length > 0) {
    	headerAlert = headerAlert[0];
		}
    if (headerAlert) {
    	var pageAlertEnabled = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].classList.contains('page-category--r19') || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].classList.contains('page-product--r23');
    	var showTopAlert = (typeof coremediaR23Settings !== 'undefined' && coremediaR23Settings.showTopAlert === true) || pageAlertEnabled;
        if (headerAlert.textContent.trim().length > 0 && showTopAlert) {
	     document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].classList.add('header-alert-visible');
	    }
    }

    headerEl.classList.add('header-r23--ready');
    setTimeout(function() {
      // evito di animare l'header al primo caricamento della pagina (quando l'utente Ã¨ in alto)
      headerEl.classList.add('header-r23--animation');
    }, window.scrollY === 0 ? 0 : 1000);
  }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function docReady(fn) {
		// see if DOM is already available
		if (document.readyState === "complete" || document.readyState === "interactive") {
			// call on next available tick
			setTimeout(fn, 1);
		} else {
			document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", fn);
		}
	} 
	docReady(function() {
		window.addToWishlistErrorMsg = 'Your selection is either incomplete or not in stock. Please be sure to supply a value for each attribute or consider a different combination of values.';
	});
</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			$(document).ready(function() {
				//if (COMMON.userId !== '-1002' && typeof COMMON.billingAddressEmail === 'undefined') {
				if (typeof COMMON.billingAddressEmail === 'undefined') {
					//TODO:
					// - COMMON.billingAddressEmail ï¿½ sempre undefined ma dovrebbe essere inizializzato e quindi esegue sempre la getProfile
					// - COMMON.userId viene cacheato in base al tipo utente quindi non posso usarlo e il cookie non si puï¿½ leggere xkï¿½ http only
					if (COMMON.personalInformation.addressType === 'ShippingAndBilling') {
						COMMON.billingAddressEmail = COMMON.personalInformation.email1;
					} else if (typeof COMMON.personalInformation.contact !== 'undefined') {
						COMMON.personalInformation.contact.forEach( function(contact) {
							if (contact.addressType === 'ShippingAndBilling') {
								COMMON.billingAddressEmail = contact.email1;
							}
						});
					}
				}
			});

<script type="text/javascript">

	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA = {

	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignIn = function (){
		window.reCaptchaValiditySignIn = false;
		if (window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn === null) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn = grecaptcha.render('signin_recaptcha', {
	            'sitekey': LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.reCaptchaKey,
	            'callback': function (response) {
	                if (LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.reCaptchaUrl !== null) {
	                	window.reCaptchaValiditySignIn = true;
	                	$('#formModalForgot').find('.cmp-input-error--recaptcha').toggleClass('hidden', window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn);
	                } else {
	                    //versione statica
	                	window.reCaptchaValiditySignIn = true;
	                	$('#formModalForgot').find('.cmp-input-error--recaptcha').toggleClass('hidden', window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn);
	                }
	            }
	        });
	    } else {
	        grecaptcha.reset(window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn);
	    }
	};
	
	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignInCheckout = function (){
		window.reCaptchaValiditySignInCheckout = false;
		if (window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInCheckout === null) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInCheckout = grecaptcha.render('signin_recaptcha_checkout', {
	            'sitekey': LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.reCaptchaKey,
	            'callback': function (response) {
	                window.reCaptchaValiditySignInCheckout = true;
	                $('#formModalForgot').find('.cmp-input-error--recaptcha').toggleClass('hidden', window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInCheckout);
	                $(document).chktR21Email('loginCheckout');
	            }
	        });
	    } else {
	        grecaptcha.reset(window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInCheckout);
	    }
	};
	
	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignInTryAtHome = function (){

	            'sitekey': LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.reCaptchaKey,

	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaLoginCommessi = function (){
		var isIpInWhitelist = $('input:hidden[name=IsIpInWhitelist]').val();
		if(isIpInWhitelist == "true") {
			window.reCaptchaValidityLoginCommessi = true;
		} else {
			window.reCaptchaValidityLoginCommessi = false;
		
			if (typeof window.reCaptchaWidgetIdLoginCommessi === 'undefined' || window.reCaptchaWidgetIdLoginCommessi === null) {
				window.reCaptchaWidgetIdLoginCommessi = grecaptcha.render('login_commessi_recaptcha', {
					'sitekey': LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.invisibleReCapcthaKey,
					'size' : 'invisible',
		            'callback': function (response) {
						COMMON.gRecResp = response;
						window.reCaptchaValidityLoginCommessi = true;
						//$('td').find('.cmp-input-error--recaptcha').toggleClass('hidden', window.reCaptchaValidityLoginCommessi);
						var a = $('#inpUser').val();
		                window.submitLoginOE(a);
		            }
		        });
		    } else {
		        grecaptcha.reset(window.reCaptchaWidgetIdLoginCommessi);
		    }
		}
	};

	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaNewsletter = function() {

		window.reCaptchaValidityNewsletter = false;
		if (typeof window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletter === 'undefined' || window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletter === null) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletter = grecaptcha.render('newsletter_recaptcha', {
				'sitekey': LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.invisibleReCapcthaKey,
				'size' : 'invisible',
				'callback': function (response) {
					COMMON.gRecResp = response;
					window.reCaptchaValidityNewsletter = true;
					$(document).footer('submitForm',$('#footerNewsletterForm'));
				}
	        });
	    } else {
	        grecaptcha.reset(window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletter);
	    }
	};

	LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaGamification = function() {
		window.reCaptchaValidityGamification = false;
		if (typeof window.reCaptchaWidgetIdGamification === 'undefined' || window.reCaptchaWidgetIdGamification === null) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdGamification = grecaptcha.render('gamification_recaptcha', {

	window.onloadCallback = function() {
		if($('#signin_recaptcha').length > 0){
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignIn = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignIn();
		}
		if($('#signup_recaptcha').length > 0) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignUp = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignUp();
		}
		if($('#modal_callmeback_recaptcha').length > 0) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdCallMeBack = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaCallMeBack();
		}
		if($('.footer-r23__newsletter__submit').length > 0) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletter = null;
			$('.footer-r23__newsletter__disclaimer').append(LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.privacyPolicyTerms);
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaNewsletter();
		}
		if($('.digital__newsetter-sign-in-button--r19').length > 0) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdNewsletterDigital = null;
			$('#digitalNewsletterForm').append(LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.privacyPolicyTerms);
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaNewsletterDigital();
		}
		/* if($('#signin_recaptcha_checkout').length > 0){
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInCheckout = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignInCheckout();
		} */
		if($('#login_commessi_recaptcha').length > 0) {
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdLoginCommessi = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaLoginCommessi();
		}
		if($('#signin_recaptcha_tryathome').length > 0){
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdSignInTryAtHome = null;
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initRecaptchaSignInTryAtHome();
		}
		var $formGamification = $('#formGamification');
		if($formGamification.length > 0){
			window.reCaptchaWidgetIdGamification = null;			
			if ($formGamification.find('[name="service"][value="eyewear"]').length > 0) {
				$formGamification.find('.footer-r23__newsletter__disclaimer').append(LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.privacyPolicyTerms);
			}
			LOADCALLBACKRECAPTCHA.initInvisibleRecaptchaGamification();
		}
	};
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function ($) {
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.guaTrackingId = 'UA-10076382-1';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.crossDomainTrackingArray = ['ferragamo.cn'];
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.currencySymbol = '&amp;#36; ';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.currencyCode = 'USD';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonical = "https://www.ferragamo.com/shop/us/en/women/womens-sale/fine-jewellery-3074457345616743418--1";
	if (B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonical === '') {
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonical = window.location.href;
	}
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonicalPath = "/shop/us/en/women/womens-sale/fine-jewellery-3074457345616743418--1";
	if (B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonicalPath === '') {
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonicalPath = window.location.pathname;
	}
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgStoreIdentifier = 'Ferragamo_US';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.shortLocale = 'en';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.Country = 'us';
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.storeId = '31150';
	if (COMMON.userType === 'G') {
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.visitorType = 'no logged';
	} else {
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.visitorType = 'logged';
	}
	//B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.visitorType = '';
	if(isMobile.any_smartphones() !== null && isMobile.any_tablets() === null){
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.Devicetype = 'mobile';
	}else if(isMobile.any_tablets() !== null){
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.Devicetype = 'tablet';
	}else{
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.Devicetype = 'desktop';
	}
	//FERRAGAMO-3885: if FRG_analytics !== 'yes', not include GA features
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled = false;
	if($.cookie('FRG_analytics') === 'yes') {
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled = true; 
	}
	//FERRAGAMO-3885: if FRG_profiling != 'yes' and FRG_analytics == 'yes', disabled GA features
	B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.allowAdFeatures = false; 
	if($.cookie('FRG_profiling') === 'yes' && $.cookie('FRG_analytics') === 'yes'){
		B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.allowAdFeatures = true; 
	}
	debug.debug(":: GUA :: init: " + JSON.stringify(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS));
});
</script>

					ga('require', 'linker');
					ga('linker:autoLink', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.crossDomainTrackingArray);
					
					
					ga('set', 'dimension1', 'eCommerce');
					ga('set', 'dimension2', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.visitorType);
					ga('set', 'dimension6', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.Devicetype);
					ga('set', 'dimension5', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.productCategoryPath);
					
					ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
					ga('set', 'anonymizeIp', true);
					ga('require', 'linkid', 'linkid.js');
					ga('require', 'ec');
					ga('set', 'currencyCode', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.currencyCode);
					ga('set', 'allowAdFeatures', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.allowAdFeatures);
					ga('send', 'pageview', B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonicalPath);
				});
			}
		});
		</script>
	
<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
		$(document).on( "headerloaded", function() {
			$("ul.main-menu__tree-list > li").one( "click", "a", function() {
				var subCategory = this.innerText.trim();
				var menuLevel = $(this).attr('qa-menu-level-id');
				var category = $(this).closest("li.main-menu__tree-first-level").find("a.main-menu__tree-link--last-open").text().trim();
				if(MAIN.responsive_r23.getBreakpoint() === 'xs' || MAIN.responsive_r23.getBreakpoint() === 'sm'){
					//mobile
					if($(this).parent().hasClass('visible-xs-block--r19')){
						ga('send', 'event', 'Menu', category, subCategory);
					}else if(menuLevel > 1) {
						category = $(this).closest('ul').siblings().text().trim();
						ga('send', 'event', 'Menu', category, subCategory);
					}
				}else{
					//desktop
					if(menuLevel > 1){
						category = $(this).closest('ul').siblings().text().trim();
					}
					if(category === ''){
					category = subCategory;
					subCategory = '';
					}
			// 		debug.debug("category:"+category+" subCategory:"+subCategory);
					ga('send', 'event', 'Menu', category, subCategory);
				}
			});
		});
	}
});

</script>

$(document).ready(function ($) {
	if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
	// 	$("ol.breadcrumb").on( "click", "ul.dropdown-menu > li > a", function() {
		$(".plp__breadcrumb-list--r19").on( "click", "li > a", function() {
			var gender = $(".plp__breadcrumb-list--r19").attr("data-parent-top-cat");
			var clickedLabel = "";
			if (gender !== undefined && gender !== "") {
				clickedLabel = gender + " " + $( this ).text().trim();
			} else {
				clickedLabel = $( this ).text().trim();
			}
	//		debug.debug(clickedLabel);
			
			var elSeparator = " | ";
	// 		var breadcrumbStep1 = $.trim( $(".ga-breadcrumb-step1").text() );
	// 		var breadcrumbStep2 = $.trim( $(".ga-breadcrumb-step2").text() );
	// 		var breadcrumbStep3 = $.trim( $(".ga-breadcrumb-step3").text() );
	// 		var allBreadcrumb = breadcrumbStep1 + elSeparator + breadcrumbStep2 + elSeparator + breadcrumbStep3;
			var allBreadcrumb = "";
			$('.plp__breadcrumb-item--r19').each(function(index,item) {
				//ciclo tutti gli elementi con class "ga-breadcrumb-step<N>" per costruire il breadcrumb intero
				if (allBreadcrumb === "" || (allBreadcrumb.lastIndexOf(elSeparator) === allBreadcrumb.length - elSeparator.length) > 0) {
					allBreadcrumb = allBreadcrumb + $(item).find('a').text().trim();
				} else {
					if(index === ($('.plp__breadcrumb-item--r19').length - 1)){
						allBreadcrumb = allBreadcrumb + elSeparator + $(item).text().trim();
					}else{
						allBreadcrumb = allBreadcrumb + elSeparator + $(item).find('a').text().trim();
					}
				}
			});
	//		debug.debug(allBreadcrumb);

			ga('send', 'event', clickedLabel, allBreadcrumb, B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgCanonicalPath);
		});
	}
});
</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function ($) {
		if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
			$(document).on( "openFilterEvent", function() {
				//traccio l'evento solo se il filtro non ï¿½ giï¿½ espanso
				var gender = $(".plp__breadcrumb-list--r19").attr("data-parent-top-cat");
				var category = $('.plp__breadcrumb-item--r19').last().text().trim();
				var categoryName = category + " " + gender + " - Filter";

				ga('send', 'event', 'Category Page', categoryName, 'Click');
			});
		}
	});
	</script>
	
	
	<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function ($) {
		if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
			$(document).on('categoryLoaded',function(){
				$("#filterBy > div.plp-filters__sticky-buttons > div.sticky-buttons > button.button-submit").on( "click", function() {
					var gender = $(".plp__breadcrumb-list--r19").attr("data-parent-top-cat");
					var category = $('.plp__breadcrumb-item--r19').last().text().trim();
					var categoryName = category + " " + gender + " - Filter Result";
					
					var numResult = $('[data-id="inStockCounter"]').last().text();
					//debug.debug(categoryName + "--" + numResult);

					ga('send', 'event', 'Category Page', categoryName, numResult);
				});
			});
		}
	});
	</script>
	
	
	<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function ($) {
		if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
			$(document).on( "click", "#collapseSortBy > ul > li > button", function() {
				var gender = $(".plp__breadcrumb-list--r19").attr("data-parent-top-cat");
				var category = $('.plp__breadcrumb-item--r19').last().text().trim();
				var categoryName = category + " " + gender + " - Sort";
				var sortName = $(this).text().trim();
		//		debug.debug(sortName + " --- " + categoryName);
		
				ga('send', 'event', 'Category Page', categoryName, sortName);
			});
		}
	});
	</script>
	
	
	<script type="text/javascript">
	
	$(document).ready(function ($) {
		if(B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.enabled){
			$(document).on('categoryLoaded',function(){
				$('li.r23-grid--list-plp__item').not('li.r23-grid--list-plp__item--core-media').on( "click", function(e) {
					var isWishlistButton = $(e.target).closest('.r23-grid--list-plp__item__product-wishlist').length > 0;
					if(!isWishlistButton) {
						var sku = $(this).find('button').data('partnumber');
						var productName = $(this).find('div.r23-grid--list-plp__item__info__product-name').text().trim();
						var position = B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.getPositionCount(this, "li.r23-grid--list-plp__item:not(li.r23-grid--list-plp__item--core-media)");
						var destUrl = $(this).find('a').attr("href");
						//debug.debug("----->sku: " + sku + " productName: " + productName + " category: " + B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.productCategoryPath + " position: " + position + " destUrl: " + destUrl);
						
						ga('ec:addProduct', {
							'id': sku,
							'name': productName,
							'brand': B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.frgStoreIdentifier,
							'category': B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.productCategoryPath,
							'position': position
						});
						ga('ec:setAction', 'click', {list: B_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS.productCategoryPath});
						ga('send', 'event', 'Category page', 'click', 'Results', {
							hitCallback: function() {
								document.location = destUrl;
							}
						});
						var id = $(this).attr('id');
						$('.category-content-r23').categoryR23("setPersistenceProductClicked", id);
					}
				});
			});
		}
	});
	</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function ($) {
		if(MAIN.responsive_r19.getBreakpoint() === 'xs'){
			var liWidths = 0;
			$('.plp-breadcrumb-r23__list__item').each(function(index,item){ 
				liWidths += $(item).outerWidth();
			});
			if(liWidths >= $('.plp-breadcrumb-r23__list__item').width()){
				var $firstLiElem = $('.plp-breadcrumb-r23__list__item')[0];
				$($firstLiElem).html('... /&nbsp;');
				$($firstLiElem).attr('disabled');
			}
		}
		$('.plp-breadcrumb-r23__list__item').css('visibility','visible');
	});	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var facetColorMap = {};
	var colorAggrValues = 'BLACK:Black|WHITE:White|BROWN:Brown|PINK:Pink|YELLOW:Yellow|VIOLET:#ee82ee|ORANGE:#ffa500|GREY:Grey|SILVER:#c0c0c0|BLUE:Blue|GOLD:#ffd700|RED:Red|GREEN:#008000|BEIGE:Beige|COLORLESS:transparent|MULTICOLOR:linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(255, 0, 0, 1) 0%, rgba(208, 222, 33, 1) 20%, rgba(63, 218, 216, 1) 40%, rgba(28, 127, 238, 1) 60%, rgba(186, 12, 248, 1) 80%, rgba(255, 0, 0, 1) 100%)';
	colorAggrValues = colorAggrValues.split('|');
	$(colorAggrValues).each(function (i, item) { 
		var color = item.split(':');
		facetColorMap[color[0].toUpperCase()] = color[1];
	});
	window.outOfStockDefaultVal = "true" === 'false' ? true : false;
